The obtain() method (line 62) acquires a canvas from a pool, and finishRecording() (line 84) completes the recording for GPU replay.\\n\\n**Rendering Flow**: ViewRootImpl.performTraversals() → measure/layout phases → performDraw() → ThreadedRenderer.draw() → RecordingCanvas records operations → GPU rendering via HardwareRenderer. The Choreographer synchronizes this entire pipeline with VSYNC signals from the display, ensuring smooth 60fps (or higher) rendering.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
